Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.INVH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.INVH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.INVI_ITEM_CODE) as SOI_ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 131652 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

Title: 
Message: Stock Query
StackTrace: SELECT om_item.item_code Item_Code,  lcs_grade_code_1 GradeCode_1, om_item.item_name Item_Description, A.item_bar_code Item_Bar_Code, A.item_price_type_1 AS PRICE1, A.item_price_type_2  AS PRICE2, ( ( lcs_stk_qty_bu + lcs_rcvd_qty_bu ) - ( lcs_issd_qty_bu + lcs_hold_qty_bu + lcs_reject_qty_bu +  lcs_overres_qty_bu + lcs_pick_qty_bu + lcs_pack_qty_bu)) AS Avail_Stock_Qty FROM   os_locn_curr_stk, om_item, om_pos_item A,  crm_om_location WHERE  om_item.item_code = A.item_code  AND om_item.item_code = lcs_item_code  AND om_item.item_frz_flag_num = 2  AND lcs_comp_code = '001'  AND lcs_locn_code = locn_code   and lcs_locn_code = '013'  AND item_pli_pl_code = 'OGENPL'  GROUP  BY om_item.item_code,  om_item.item_name, A.item_bar_code,  locn_name,  om_item.item_uom_code,  lcs_grade_code_1,  lcs_grade_code_2,  A.item_pli_pl_code,  A.item_price_type_1,  A.item_price_type_2,  lcs_stk_qty_bu,  lcs_rcvd_qty_bu,  lcs_issd_qty_bu,  lcs_hold_qty_bu,  lcs_reject_qty_bu,  lcs_overres_qty_bu,  lcs_pick_qty_bu,  lcs_pack_qty_bu,  lcs_resv_qty_bu,  om_item.item_anly_code_01,  om_item.item_anly_code_02 HAVING SUM(( ( lcs_stk_qty_bu + lcs_rcvd_qty_bu ) -  ( lcs_issd_qty_bu + lcs_hold_qty_bu  + lcs_reject_qty_bu +  lcs_overres_qty_bu  + lcs_pick_qty_bu +  lcs_pack_qty_bu )  - lcs_resv_qty_bu )) > 0 ORDER  BY locn_name, item_code

Title: 
Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.INVH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.INVH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.INVI_ITEM_CODE) as SOI_ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress,  nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 131655 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.INVH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.INVH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.INVI_ITEM_CODE) as SOI_ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress,  nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 131655 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.INVI_ITEM_CODE) as SOI_ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress,  nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxamt.  nvl((select ITED_TED_RATE from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxpercentage  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 131656 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

Message: Direct Invoice Report Query

as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.INVH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.INVH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.INVI_ITEM_CODE) as SOI_ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress,  nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxamt,  nvl((select ITED_TED_RATE from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxpercentage  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 131058 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

Message: Sales Return Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.CSRH_NO ,to_char( b.CSRH_DT,'DD/MM/YYYY') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.CSRH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.CSRH_CUST_CODE) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.CSRH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.CSRH_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.CSRH_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.CSRH_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.CSRH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.CSRH_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.CSRH_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.CSRH_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.CSRH_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.CSRI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.CSRI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.CSRI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.CSRI_RATE as ItmPrice , a.CSRI_QTY as ItmQty, a.CSRI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((SELECT ITED_FC_AMT from OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID= a.CSRI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM  from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((SELECT ITED_FC_AMT from OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID= a.CSRI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM  from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,CSRH_SM_CODE as salesman,CSRH_FLEX_03 as pm_cust_no, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.CSRI_ITEM_CODE) as ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress  from  OT_CUST_SALE_RET_HEAD b,OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM a,om_location c,om_address d where b.CSRH_NO = 130210 and b.CSRH_SYS_ID = a.CSRI_CSRH_SYS_ID and b.CSRH_LOCN_CODE = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code

Title: 
Message: Sales Return Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.CSRH_NO ,to_char( b.CSRH_DT,'DD/MM/YYYY') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, case nvl(b.CSRH_FLEX_03,0) when '0' then (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.CSRH_CUST_CODE) else (select PM_PATIENT_NAME from om_patient_master where PM_CUST_NO = b.CSRH_FLEX_03) end as CustName, b.CSRH_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.CSRH_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.CSRH_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.CSRH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.CSRH_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.CSRH_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.CSRH_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.CSRH_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.CSRI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.CSRI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.CSRI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.CSRI_RATE as ItmPrice , a.CSRI_QTY as ItmQty, a.CSRI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((SELECT ITED_FC_AMT from OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID= a.CSRI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM  from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((SELECT ITED_FC_AMT from OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID= a.CSRI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM  from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,CSRH_SM_CODE as salesman,CSRH_FLEX_03 as pm_cust_no, (select ITEM_BL_LONG_NAME_1 from om_item where ITEM_CODE=a.CSRI_ITEM_CODE) as ITEM_NAME_ARABIC, c.LOCN_BL_NAME as locnArabicName, d.ADDR_LINE_4||' '||d.ADDR_LINE_5 as locnArabicAddress,  nvl((SELECT ITED_FC_AMT from OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID= a.CSRI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM  from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TAX')),0) as taxamt  from  OT_CUST_SALE_RET_HEAD b,OT_CUST_SALE_RET_ITEM a,om_location c,om_address d where b.CSRH_NO = 130211 and b.CSRH_SYS_ID = a.CSRI_CSRH_SYS_ID and b.CSRH_LOCN_CODE = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code
